  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a0f84ff6-7773-4e53-bb77-545231ee6d7b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer8304861444988980361"><b>18 hrs and 15 mins </b> <br/><br/>Lieutenant Alexander Colton and February Owens were high-school sweethearts.   <span id="freeText8304861444988980361" style="display:none"><b>18 hrs and 15 mins </b> <br /><br />Lieutenant Alexander Colton and February Owens were high-school sweethearts. Everyone in their small town knew from the moment they met they were meant for each other. But something happened, and Feb broke Colt's heart; then she turned wild, and tragedy struck. Colt meted out revenge against the man who brought Feb low, but even though Colt risked it all for her, Feb turned her back on him and left town.<br /><br />Fifteen years later Feb comes back to help run the family bar. But there's so much water under the bridge separating her and Colt, everyone knows they'll never get back together - until someone starts hacking up people in Feb's life. Colt is still Colt, and Feb is still Feb, so the town watches as Colt goes all out to find the murderer while trying to keep Feb safe. As the bodies pile up, the feds move in, and a twisting, turning story unravels, exposing a very sick man who has claimed numerous victims. Along the way Feb and Colt battle their enduring attraction and the beautiful but lost history that weaves them together.<br /><br />©2014 Kristen Ashley; (P)2015 Audible Inc.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Hi..I just reread it again... just because I Iove At peace and kinda like read this first...So I think you should read it... Angst?! well I have to sa<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Hi..I just reread it again... just because I Iove At peace and kinda like read this first...So I think you should read it... Angst?! well I have to say for me there is not to much of angst certainly I have read books with some major angst and this is not one of them... for me is more of second chance romance with mature characters..and sure there is drama with this whole murder thing but I don't know if you have read KA books.. it's her typical work..at least first three books in series... and maybe Hold on( final book of the series) are worth reading... Enjoy! and now I am really curious did you liked it?? <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2783991827516720599"><br/><b>My Review -</b><br/><br/>Keepin’ it short…<br/><br/><i>For You</i> is the first book in Kristen Ashley’s <i>The Burg</i> series, and one of the most intense books I’ve read. Crazy bitches, nut job exes, psychotic killers, drunks, and addicts… devoted cops, amazing women, lots of action, romance, humor and plenty of burn up the pages sex… this book has it all. Seriously. Has. It. All. Colt and Feb are fantastic characters with an awesome supporting cast!<br/><br/>I don’t know how she does it but, book after book, without fail, Kristen Ashley d</span>
  <span id="freeText2783991827516720599" style="display:none"><br /><b>My Review -</b><br /><br />Keepin’ it short…<br /><br /><i>For You</i> is the first book in Kristen Ashley’s <i>The Burg</i> series, and one of the most intense books I’ve read. Crazy bitches, nut job exes, psychotic killers, drunks, and addicts… devoted cops, amazing women, lots of action, romance, humor and plenty of burn up the pages sex… this book has it all. Seriously. Has. It. All. Colt and Feb are fantastic characters with an awesome supporting cast!<br /><br />I don’t know how she does it but, book after book, without fail, Kristen Ashley delivers stories that grab hold and don’t let go, and heroes and heroines who come to mind time and time again, and I am sooooo happy to be on board the KA Train!<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2783991827516720599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_989676142" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/989676142" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/989676142?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer989676142" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5028094063509110342"><b>5 utterly beautiful and heartbreaking STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417080516i/12208432.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>WOW...just WOW!<br/><br/>I'm sure at this point a lot of you are tired of my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> reading spree, but I can't stop and you just have to deal. I'm sorry. <br/>Good news is, this is one hell of a book and I honestly think <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480-for-you' rel='nofollow noopener'>For You</a> has something for everyone. An epic love story, mystery that keeps you at the edge of your seat, suspense and tissue moments that break your heart</span>
  <span id="freeText5028094063509110342" style="display:none"><b>5 utterly beautiful and heartbreaking STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417080516i/12208432.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>WOW...just WOW!<br><br>I'm sure at this point a lot of you are tired of my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> reading spree, but I can't stop and you just have to deal. I'm sorry. <br>Good news is, this is one hell of a book and I honestly think <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480-for-you" rel="nofollow noopener">For You</a> has something for everyone. An epic love story, mystery that keeps you at the edge of your seat, suspense and tissue moments that break your heart.<br><br>With my growing KA experience I can honestly say this is not like the others. And I suspect the whole series will be very enjoyable. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve moved on, Colt.”<br>“Bullshit, Feb, you’re stuck, same as me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Let's start with the most important thing:<br><br><i><b>February Owens</b> and <b>Alexander Colton</b> are meant to be together.</i><br><br>There are no two ways about it. They've known each other since forever and have always been a little bit more than friends until they eventually got together as teenagers.<br><br>When Feb was twenty years and Colt twenty-two years old <u>something</u> happened and the couple everyone was rooting for broke up - out of the blue, from one day to another - all over.<br><br>February went wild, got into a lot of trouble and eventually married the wrong guy. The guy who turned out to be violent and a complete asshole. The whole thing turned into revenge dished out by no other than Colt, a divorce and Feb leaving town.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417552762ra/12411615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know that's a lot of information, but that's actually already disclosed in the blurb, so don't worry. In the grand scheme of things that's very little input.<br><br>But forget about the past for a little while and FAST FORWARD twenty years, that's where all the drama lies...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Seems to be there’s advantage to be taken, son, and ain’t no one in a hundred mile radius would blame you for takin’ it.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>At this point Feb has been back in town for two years and today she has one hell of a crap day. Although finding a friend in the alley behind your bar - murdered - will do that to you. And the day takes a turn for the worse when the former love of her life, her high school sweetheart and lead Detective Alexander Colton arrives. And then the following days turn into a much bigger mess when even more dead bodies turn up...all seemingly connected to dear February Owens.<br><br>What follows is a thrilling murder hunt, two damaged people trying to unravel the past in order to solve an atrocious crime and their future at the same time.<br><i>For You</i> is a beautiful and very complex story; with a lot of secrets, unknown players and unfortunately...death. <br><br>I'm just going to confess here...yes, I cried. *sniffs* That doesn't happen very often, but I cried and maybe I had a hormonal day, but I was moved and I'm not afraid to share. ;D Apparently Kristen Ashley can do that to me and I won't complain. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Lonely’s a different kind of pain, it doesn’t hurt as bad as heartbreak. I preferred it and embraced it ‘cause I reckoned it was one or the other.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Feb is a pretty strong character and she did the best she could with the cards she was dealt. Life just doesn't always turn out the way you want it to. What I like most about her is the taste in music. She sure knows what to listen to.<br><br>Colt...*sigh*, he is kind of awesome. He does have this perfect guy reputation in town and for all intents and purposes he does live up to the hype. Not many guys can do that. I love his conviction and determination. <br><br>Both characters are very well developed and bring a rich background, lots of family and drama. That's one thing I really like about KA books. Thanks to the length and Ms. Ashley's love for detail we get some very rounded worlds that feel so real you can almost touch it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388806981ra/7934075.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>For You</i> is a second chance story and I couldn't be happier about it. While reading this truly amazing book I came to the conclusion that second chance stories are one of my all time favourite romance tropes. It's so cheesy and predictable, but I adore it and this one was so well executed and the whole back story and murder mystery just made it all together perfect.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Despite the mayhem happening all around I really appreciated the MC's rational and mature actions. At no point was I annoyed or frustrated by Feb or Cold. In all fairness they made their mistakes a long time ago and fortunately for us they have learned a lot since then. It's really refreshing to see characters taking a breath, thinking about their actions and making good choices as a result.<br><br>And I have to say one more thing. At about 80% it hit me like a freight train...Colt is not my all time favourite book boyfriend and Feb is not my favourite book heroine - but together Colt and Feb are one of my all time favourite couples. I can't even say why it's just a feeling...they fit so well and it's such a joy to see their story unfold. And I didn't want it to end.<br><br>Also, Fleetwood Mac! If you read the book and don't know what I'm talking about...well, then I can't help you anyway 'cause there is no cure for bad taste in music.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He was hearing Stevie Nicks singing in his head when Colt fell asleep in the bed, in the house, with the woman at his side that life meant him to have. After waiting for forty-four years, for the fifth night in a row, Alexander Colton was finally living the life he was meant to be living.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>**So so sorry, this took forever to write. But better late than never. ;P<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer347967972" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16321547741932169879"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260074i/11924047._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Man Colt/Alec.. all bad-ass detective</u>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260074i/11924048._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"You know, long time ago, I looked it up," She told him.<br/>"What?" Colt asked.<br/>"Your name," she told him, her voice soft, her eyes on his unwavering and he held his breath, knowing what was coming was going to strike deep and he wasn't wrong.<br/>"Alexander," she said, "means warrior, defender. Colton, colt," she smiled, "well, we all know a colt's got so much energy, always beautiful little things, strong, fast, all of 'em gonna grow up to be something magn</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16321547741932169879" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260074i/11924047._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>My Man Colt/Alec.. all bad-ass detective</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260074i/11924048._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You know, long time ago, I looked it up," She told him.<br>"What?" Colt asked.<br>"Your name," she told him, her voice soft, her eyes on his unwavering and he held his breath, knowing what was coming was going to strike deep and he wasn't wrong.<br>"Alexander," she said, "means warrior, defender. Colton, colt," she smiled, "well, we all know a colt's got so much energy, always beautiful little things, strong, fast, all of 'em gonna grow up to be something magnificent."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>My Feb</u>
</b><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/543/doutzenkroesjeansadsba5.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380712i/737663._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Her jaw tilts for Alec:<br>I used to do it because it made him smile at me, a smile I hadn't seen in years, a smile that others saw and it was handsome so I was sure they liked it, at least the girls. But they didn't get it. They didn't understand, it not being directed at them, what that smile could do. The power of it. it was like every time he smiled he'd opened a chest of treasure and said. "All this is yours."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/843/kittyiv.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380712i/737664._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>What can I possibly say about KA... I love it. This is one of my favorite series of hers. It's a little bit darker than her usual stuff... bordering on her Colorado Mountain Series but much more twisted. I remember when I read it the first time it gave me nervous heart palpitations. Re-reading my 2nd favorite book of this series with my Smut-ateers.... I love it!<br><br>It is darker than all her other series and because of that it is heart breaking. I sobbed through the book, because life is cruel and in a small town you find the psychopathic assholes and bitches. But life is sweet too because you have so many good people at your back.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260116i/11924050._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="524" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story of Alec and Feb is a sad one... sweethearts since children. Torn apart waaaaay too young and brought together 22 years later by the same thing that torn them apart. <br><br>KA truly knows her stuff in alpha males, bitchy females and family that will lay down anything for you. And by family I mean anyone who is brought into a fold just because they either suffered through so much but has true goodness at heart (Cheryl &amp; Darryl). I have no idea where KA gets all this from and honestly don't care just as long as she keeps writing and providing my book Crack for me.<br><br>Truly amazing! Please read it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260116i/11924051._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="690" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You got in, Colt," I said and watched, super close, as his eyes opened and his hands tightened on my neck, no squeeze this time, they stayed tight and I couldn't feel the pad of every finger pressing into my skin. "Few days ago, you got in. I didn't let you in, you just got in." finally I lifted my hands to his chest and bunched his shirt in my fingers. "I wanna lock you there," I whispered scared to death but sharing it all, hiding nothing, giving him everything, fighting the hitch in my voice that my tears were threatening. "Lock you up tight inside me, babe, and never let you out."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>KA AT HER FINEST:</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>He had no idea why God decided to place him, at birth, in hell only to lead him to salvation in kindergarten. Though he suspected if he hadn't experienced hell, he wouldn't have understood salvation.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Sometimes, it's rare, but sometimes... men learn,"</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Couple things came up."<br>"I gave your table away, Colt, an hour ago."<br>"Got another one?"<br>"Colt-"<br>Stavros heard Colt cut in. "<b>SPOILER!!!</b>" Stavros sucked in breath at this long awaited, very welcome, unbelievably happy news and Colt finished. "Now, you got a table of what?"<br>Stavros grinned into the phone. "Don't got one, I'll build one."</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="16321547741932169879" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_243249345" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243249345" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243249345?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243249345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13210321972726463664"><b> <i> “… she tipped her head back and in his ear, she whispered, “Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.” </i> </b><br/><br/>Woah! What a roller-coaster of a book!! It went from creepy to intense to hot ‘n’ steamy to sweet to sad to beautiful… it had twists and turns and a story built in layers forward as well as dug in layers backwards…. quite the ride!! And I loved it!<br/><br/>So the back story that you go into this book knowing from the blurb is that Alexander Colton and Febuary Owens w</span>
  <span id="freeText13210321972726463664" style="display:none"><b> <i> “… she tipped her head back and in his ear, she whispered, “Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.” </i> </b><br><br>Woah! What a roller-coaster of a book!! It went from creepy to intense to hot ‘n’ steamy to sweet to sad to beautiful… it had twists and turns and a story built in layers forward as well as dug in layers backwards…. quite the ride!! And I loved it!<br><br>So the back story that you go into this book knowing from the blurb is that Alexander Colton and Febuary Owens were always meant to be together – they were together growing up, together in high school, everyone knew they were destined for each other… but something happened and Feb left Colt. No one knows why, but now, 20 years later, the story begins.<br><br>Right from the start, the tone of this book is grittier, more intense, and more serious than some of KA’s other series (especially considering it starts off at a chilling, grisly murder crime scene at Feb’s bar that Colt, now a cop, comes to investigate), but its still pure, brilliant KA writing that sucks you right into the world. I love that her writing style is just so familiar to me, its like coming home to start one of her books – such a wonderful feeling. LOVE!!<br><br>At the scene of the gruesome murder, the reader is introduced to Feb and Colt and their shared and, at the time, unknown history. As the reader, we know that whatever happened to them years ago was heart breaking and sad, but we don’t know exactly what it is.<br><br>Its clear that, throughout all the years of separation, neither Feb nor Cold have let go of their feelings for each other, but at the same time, aren’t able to give into them, leaving you wracking your brain trying to figure out what could possibly have ever come between a couple so clearly meant for each other.<br><br>Naturally, of course, there is a way found for Feb to end up moving in with Colt (completely platonically, of course, *nods seriously*.. for protection. *continues nodding* mmhmm.. we all know where this is gonna lead now don’t we? *grin*) and one thing leads to another and soon they are on their way to an adorably swoony reunion &lt;3<br><br><b> One thing I loved about this story was how much it really highlights that if the love is pure and real, no amount of years of separation will ever really dull it. Totally beautiful concept. </b><br><br><i> “There’s no words to explain how big it was, what Colt and I had, or how much it hurts when something that big in your life is swept away, or how empty that place is that he once filled, or how impossible it is to find something to fill it…” </i> <br><br>The more Colt and Feb came together, the more I began to squee and sigh over them, but remember that throughout it all there is the under current of mystery with not knowing who the killer is, and with waiting to figure out what happened in their past.<br><br>But once things start to build for them, oooooooohhh boy does the HOTNESS begin!! Nothing like a build up of 20 years to make the sex fan-yourself intense!! And once Alpha Colt has claim to his girl, his pulls out all the swoony, bossy, possessive stops while at the same time making my heart melt and go awwwww I just loved seeing the two of them come back together again *dreamy sigh*<br><br><i> <b> “Your mother doesnt fuck around,” Colt remarked.<br>“I hope you didn’t have anything in there that was precious.”<br>Colt looked at her and said, ”The only things precious in my life breathe.” </b></i> <br><br>*swoon* freaking LOVE that line!!<br><br>The psycho murderer in this is “without a moral compass” and just totally way-the-freaking-hell creepy in a deeeeeeply chilling way – making me alternately shudder and go ewwwwwww. This one is actually smart, disturbed, who has thought out what they were doing. Have I mentioned creepy and chilling yet?? The murders are very interconnected, personal and now the cover of the book makes sense to me *shudder*<br><br>The story is told in alternating POVs, but it was Colt’s POV that was the most interesting to me because he was not only trying to solve the murder, but was also trying to piece together the puzzle of his and Feb’s past and trying to understand how, somehow, the murder and those events might be tied together.<br><br>Of course, I won’t tell you what it is, but I will say that my heart was POUNDING when the explanation comes out! Its told from Colt’s POV and you experience the shock and realization as everything clicks into place for him. Its huge!! I just love moments like that in books!<br><br>The wonderful thing is that once the muck and turmoil of the past was finally figured out, it left Colt and Feb open to go for what they both really wanted all along – each other <br><br><i> “Romeo and Juliet, say they didn’t die but Juliet got pissed and took off. Everyone would know it was Romeo and Juliet, would always be Romeo and Juliet, even if later Romeo hooked up with Nancy. No one ever heard of Nancy, doesn’t even sound right, Romeo and Nancy. Everyone knows Romeo’s meant to be with Juliet. Even if Romeo loved Nancy, Nancy would always know she was never Juliet.” </i> <br><br>I actually really loved that neither Colt nor Feb were perfect characters. Yes, in a perfect world, if they made perfect decisions, then the decisions they made in their past would have been different. But they both fucked up. They both paid the price. They both knew it, admitted it. And they were both ready to move on and not dwell in the past, but to live in the present. I really admired that about both of them and I love that they had a second chance at their love.<br><br><i> <b> “Then in my ear, he said, “I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried… Who knows, baby? We had all that time together, I coulda got used to it, learned to take it for granted.” His arms gave me a squeeze. “Now, that’ll never happen.” </b></i> <br><br>And I just can’t say enough how much I JUST FREAKING LOVE Kristen Ashley’s writing style!! I think she could make a scene about paint drying riveting (not that I’m at all comparing this book to that, just saying that she works magic into her words). Her writing style totally connects you to the story, and the characters, no matter what is going on in the scene.<br><br>The book didn’t make me cry ever although I did get a little chocked up twice near the end, which, as usual, left me smiling, awww-ing and grinning… there wasn’t an epilogue in this book but KA writes the best endings and this was was no exception.<br><br>An amazing start to this series… I cannot WAIT to get to book 2 since everyone is RAVING about it!! *squee*<br><br>**oh and can I just throw a shout-out out to the character of Graham Reece who was only in a few scenes of this book but TOTALLY made me SWOON!!! I am SO looking forward to his book (which is the next book in the Colorado Mountain series). YAY!<br><br>4.5+ stars<br><br>How I see Colt and Feb: <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379777049i/363217._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13210321972726463664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/262376829?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=family-dynamic">family-dynamic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=exhausting-read">exhausting-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=outstanding-epilogue">outstanding-epilogue</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262376829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12098586164557157034"><b>Solid 4 stars</b><br/><br/>Wow! What an intense and gripping read! <br/><br/><i>For You</i> is a intricately written, multi-layered suspense story with a great romance and a cast of fantastic characters. The plot is full of suspense, drama, heartache, passion, steamy sex scenes, and one seriously crazy, out-of-his-mind, psycho killer. <br/><br/><i>For You</i> had my attention from the first page to the last. Mystery and suspense seemed to be the main focus of the book rather than Kristen Ashley's typical romance centered plots—although, there</span>
  <span id="freeText12098586164557157034" style="display:none"><b>Solid 4 stars</b><br /><br />Wow! What an intense and gripping read! <br /><br /><i>For You</i> is a intricately written, multi-layered suspense story with a great romance and a cast of fantastic characters. The plot is full of suspense, drama, heartache, passion, steamy sex scenes, and one seriously crazy, out-of-his-mind, psycho killer. <br /><br /><i>For You</i> had my attention from the first page to the last. Mystery and suspense seemed to be the main focus of the book rather than Kristen Ashley's typical romance centered plots—although, there was plenty of romance as well. <br /><br />The "second chance at romance" storyline between Colt and Feb was touching, heartbreaking, and very emotional. My heart broke for these two wonderful characters and the injustices done to them. These two were destined to be together, and when that finally happens for them, there was genuine joy in my heart.  <br /><br />As with all Kristen Ashley books, the epilogue was full of happiness, memories, and lots of heart and soul. This one left me with a big smile on my face. I find myself as anxious to read her epilogues as I am to read the main story. That how amazing they are. <br /><br /><i>For You</i> is another fantastic book by Kristen Ashley and one I definitely recommend. <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer399695662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3609352436739878997"><b>4.5 Stars... For You </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/aefa2006-03d0-4c73-a5a9-7b691794dcff_zps02e2dd37.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749770.jpg' alt=' photo aefa2006-03d0-4c73-a5a9-7b691794dcff_zps02e2dd37.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Murder, suspense, romance, love, betrayal, reconciliation, friendship, sex, and a second chance at your one true love... this book had it all! <br/><br/><b>Lonely’s a different kind of pain, it doesn’t hurt as bad as heartbreak. I preferred it and embraced it ‘cause I reckoned it was one or another.</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0dd7b818-6e08-4b33-9a5d-8dcc94c9cf74_zps3a913feb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749771.jpg' alt=' photo 0dd7b818-6e08-4b33-9a5d-8dcc94c9cf74_zps3a913feb.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
</b> <br/><br/>February ‘Feb’ Owens was in love once. With Alexander Colton. They have a history, a past. Something h</span>
  <span id="freeText3609352436739878997" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars... For You </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/aefa2006-03d0-4c73-a5a9-7b691794dcff_zps02e2dd37.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749770.jpg" alt=" photo aefa2006-03d0-4c73-a5a9-7b691794dcff_zps02e2dd37.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Murder, suspense, romance, love, betrayal, reconciliation, friendship, sex, and a second chance at your one true love... this book had it all! <br><br><b>Lonely’s a different kind of pain, it doesn’t hurt as bad as heartbreak. I preferred it and embraced it ‘cause I reckoned it was one or another.</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0dd7b818-6e08-4b33-9a5d-8dcc94c9cf74_zps3a913feb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749771.jpg" alt=" photo 0dd7b818-6e08-4b33-9a5d-8dcc94c9cf74_zps3a913feb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
</b> <br><br>February ‘Feb’ Owens was in love once. With Alexander Colton. They have a history, a past. Something happened between them when Feb was 20 and Alec was 22- that was nearly 22 years ago. Feb left town. They both tried to move on. Feb has been back for a few years helping her brother Morrie (who happens to be Alec’s best friend) run her family’s bar. Alec, who goes by Colt, is a lieutenant in that same town. They have been pretty much avoiding each other the past few years, but when a psycho killer starts hacking people up in their small town, they both find themselves involved. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/4d415578-74ed-4413-8d48-e2269db98524_zps4f0ee0f8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749772.jpg" alt=" photo 4d415578-74ed-4413-8d48-e2269db98524_zps4f0ee0f8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Colt and Feb both obviously have some unresolved feelings for each other. They were high school sweethearts, everyone in town loved them together. It was such a shock when they broke up. They both tried to move on, but you never really get over your one true love. <br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i>“There’s no words to explain how big it was, what Colt and I had, or how much it hurts when something that big in your life is swept away, or how empty that place is that he once filled, or how impossible it is to find something to fill it.” </i>
  </b>
</p><br><br>As Colt and Feb start spending more time together, their romance is rekindled. Everyone in town is rooting for these two to be together, especially Feb’s parents. Finding out what transpired between them all those years ago was devastating. They had an intense relationship and some fierce chemistry. They are moving forward, trying to pick up where they left off and make up for lost time. <br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i>“Like it right now or not, Feb, couple of days ago, you gave yourself back to me. You think I’m lettin’ that go, think again because, baby, your fucking wrong.”<br><br>“I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried... Who knows, baby? We had all that time together, I coulda got used to it, leaned to take it for granted. Now, that’ll never happen.”</i>
  </b>
</p><br><br>Things are going well for the couple, but there is that pesky matter that is Denny. The serial killer on the lose that is completely obsessed with Feb. He wants to ‘take care’ of everyone who he has perceived to have wronged Feb over the years. Colt being the biggest of all. The last 10% was intense... <br><br>This plot was suspenseful, but it was also sweet, funny and sexy. The perfect combination. The characters were lovable. Colt was always trying to support and protect Feb, he was such a loving, sweet and sexy man! They were both trying to make up for all the time they lost. I especially loved Feb’s parents, her brother was great too. The story was a long one, but it didn’t drag- kept me interested. The ending left me completely satisfied, couldn’t wipe the smile off my face!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e216e721-9b20-4def-aaee-4366a523ed63_zpsce184025.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388906i/749773.jpg" alt=" photo e216e721-9b20-4def-aaee-4366a523ed63_zpsce184025.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am pretty sure I will read and love anything written by this author! This book was no exception. Kristen Ashely can write some wonderful alpha males, heroines, and the most perfect endings ever! Looking forward to reading many more of her books!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>“The only precious things in life breathe.”</i>
</b><br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer945857699" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2093190048335714739"><b>For You</b> is the first book in The Burg Series by Kristen Ashley and there is only one word to describe it...PERFECTION! KA offers a delicious read full of action, suspense, and second chances. Feb and Colt are two characters that were meant to be together. When a stalker wants to get his hands on February, Colt (the town's smoking hot detective) is there to protect her. But when Colt and Feb are brought together again, the high school sweethearts are reminded of why they are meant to be together.</span>
  <span id="freeText2093190048335714739" style="display:none"><b>For You</b> is the first book in The Burg Series by Kristen Ashley and there is only one word to describe it...PERFECTION! KA offers a delicious read full of action, suspense, and second chances. Feb and Colt are two characters that were meant to be together. When a stalker wants to get his hands on February, Colt (the town's smoking hot detective) is there to protect her. But when Colt and Feb are brought together again, the high school sweethearts are reminded of why they are meant to be together. But can they overcome the demons of their past?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481435727ra/21421383.gif" width='“400"' height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Told in dual POV, <b>For You</b> is one of those KA books that I could read over and over again. The relationships between the characters are strong, and Colt and Feb have an intense connection. The action and suspense factor is high and paired with the sexy steam between the two main characters, and voila you have a perfect blend. <br><br>I highly recommend this read to anyone who enjoys suspense and romance. This is one EPIC love story that you do not want to miss! <br><br>*This is a BR with my Shhlutty sister Anna!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481436285i/21421415._SX540_.jpg" width='“200"' height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481435812i/21421386._SX540_.gif" width='“"' height="25" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481435812i/21421386._SX540_.gif" width='“"' height="25" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481435812i/21421386._SX540_.gif" width='“"' height="25" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~First read in May 2014~<br><br>4.5<br>Another home run for KA! I am just NEVER disappointed. The only reason this book isn't a perfect 5 for me is because there were so many secondary characters that it was hard sometimes to keep everyone straight. I found myself having to reread sections and even go back to other parts in the book to make sure that I knew who was who and what was up...but then again that just supports the whole small town busy body buzz! <br>Good action and a timeless love story. Watching Alec and Feb reconnect after being ripped apart over a misunderstanding was unforgettable! <br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_467676506" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467676506" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467676506?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24922709-for-you">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">It's KA . . . </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-book-boy-is-mine">the-book-boy-is-mine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=creeptastic">creeptastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=for-when-i-hate-everything">for-when-i-hate-everything</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-heart-wants-what-the">the-heart-wants-what-the</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467676506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9007432367476904159">So . . . here's the thing about KA . . . <br/><br/>KA writes stories about people that live in small towns. Even if they don't <i>actually</i> live in a small town, her books still have that small town feel: everyone grew up together, everyone knows everyone else's business, people look out for each other, no one gets lost in the crush of life, etc.<br/><br/>I absolutely adore her books, and since I first discovered them a couple of years ago, they've become my failsafe for book hangovers.<br/><br/>THE 'BURG series in particular is</span>
  <span id="freeText9007432367476904159" style="display:none">So . . . here's the thing about KA . . . <br><br>KA writes stories about people that live in small towns. Even if they don't <i>actually</i> live in a small town, her books still have that small town feel: everyone grew up together, everyone knows everyone else's business, people look out for each other, no one gets lost in the crush of life, etc.<br><br>I absolutely adore her books, and since I first discovered them a couple of years ago, they've become my failsafe for book hangovers.<br><br>THE 'BURG series in particular is one of my favorites. They're romantic suspense, but they read more like an episode of CRIMINAL MINDS . . . one of the episodes of CRIMINAL MINDS with a really creepy serial killer. Maybe that's normal for romantic suspense and I haven't read enough to know it, but most of the romantic suspense that I've read is more of the amateur sleuthing variety. KA has books like that too, but THE 'BURG . . . is an altogether different animal.<br><br>An altogether different and creeptastic animal. <br><br>February Owens and Alec Colton were part of a love story that had it continued uninterrupted, would have been the stuff of legends. But when they were in there early 20s, something happened and Feb walked away. She spent the next 15 years traveling from small town to small town, settling only temporarily, until it was time for her to move on again. Then two years ago, her parent's retired from the family business, and she moved back home to help her brother.<br><br>The book begins with February finding a dead body in the alley behind the family BAR&lt;-----how fun is that? The family bar, not the dead body.<br><br>And not just <i>any</i> dead body . . . the hacked-up (like, literally, with a hatchet) body of one of her childhood friends. And she's not doing too great when Colt shows-up, who is, of course, a detective, which is how they get thrown back into each other's path after years of avoidance. <br><br>Not the best of circumstances . . . and trust me . . . it gets worse.<br><br>But it's obvious that Feb and Colt are supposed to be together. They just have to figure out who thinks they're doing Feb a favor by killing off people from her past. <br><br>Like I said--CREEPTASTIC.<br><br>This is the third time I've read this, but it's the first time I've reviewed it, and while I was reading, I was thinking about what I could say about it, and I was struck by how . . . completely improbable the plot was. <br><br>And if I hadn't been deliberately thinking about what was happening/had happened, it still wouldn't have occurred to me.<br><br>B/c <i>that</i> is the thing about KA. Her books have a way of sneaking past all your red flags, causing you to make allowances for her books that you would NEVER make under any other circumstances. And half of the time you don't even realize you're doing it.<br><br>She's like a ninja.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402261081ra/9914186.gif" width="196" height="116" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You become so completely immersed in her storytelling that you never stop to consider how unlikely whatever it is she's selling is. It <i>did</i> happen, by golly. <br><br>And it. Was. A-W-E-S-O-M-E.<br><br>Her alphas are alpha, her quirky heroines are quirky, her secondaries are fantastic, and her HEAs are all that HEAs should be. <br><br>B/c really . . . what's the point otherwise? You don't read KA b/c you want to brag to your pompous literary friends about the next nobel prize winning novel you just read (and if you read anything with that goal in mind, go away, I don't like you). You read KA b/c for once, you want a sure thing. You want to swoon over the kind of alpha that doesn't hesitate in slamming you against a wall b/c he knows you'll like it. Just like he knows how to handle a firearm, and has a motorcycle, and hasn't starting losing his hair or going to seed, even if he IS close to 40.<br><br>Just roll with it. It will make you happy, and isn't that what books are supposed to do? <br><br>I think so.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9007432367476904159" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer">Jennifer</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_960965273" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/960965273" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/960965273?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer960965273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4685901288588519455"><b>The KA reading continues at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles</a></b><br/><br/>I do love my KA fixes with these ladies and it was so great so spend a little time with Colt and Feb again.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>The first books I read by Kristen Ashley (KA) were her Fantasyland Series and I was worried that her uber alpha males would not translate well into her contemporary fiction. I WAS WRONG!!! At least in this book, perhaps it was because she toned it down a litt</span>
  <span id="freeText4685901288588519455" style="display:none"><b>The KA reading continues at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a></b><br /><br />I do love my KA fixes with these ladies and it was so great so spend a little time with Colt and Feb again.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</i>
</blockquote><br />The first books I read by Kristen Ashley (KA) were her Fantasyland Series and I was worried that her uber alpha males would not translate well into her contemporary fiction. I WAS WRONG!!! At least in this book, perhaps it was because she toned it down a little but I absolutely ADORED Colt. Sure there is a psycho out there killing anyone from February’s past that he feels did her wrong and that was in intriguing part to the story but the other part about Colt and February reuniting after being separated for twenty years was what really hooked me from the beginning. <br /><br /><i>“There’s no words to explain how big it was, what Colt and I had, or how much it hurts when something that big in your life is swept away, or how empty that place is that he once filled, or how impossible it is to find something to fill it.”</i><br /><br />Living in their small town everyone seems to know everything about anything. So when the split between Colt and Feb happened no one understood it, they were meant to be, everyone knew that. Feb couldn’t handle the whole town knowing all of her business so she left. Both of them have tried to fill their lives apart but it is just a shadow of what it could have been and they both know it, and the whole town seems to know it too.<br /><br /><i>“Romeo and Juliet, say they didn’t die but Juliet got pissed and took off. Everyone would know it was Romeo and Juliet, would always be Romeo and Juliet, even if later Romeo hooked up with Nancy. No one ever heard of Nancy, doesn’t even sound right, Romeo and Nancy. Everyone knows Romeo’s meant to be with Juliet. Even if Romeo loved Nancy, Nancy would always know she was never Juliet”</i><br /><br />Now, thrown into each other’s lives again they have a second chance to see if things could be different. That is if they can keep each other alive and figure out who is chopping up people from Feb’s past. But that means they have to revisit their own past and figure out what really happened to them so long ago.<br /><br />I enjoyed so many things about this story. The small town feel, the way that the relationship between Feb and Colt progressed, Feb’s family and how they all came around her to protect her. I even liked the backstory to the crackpot who is focused on Feb and the connection they had. My one and only complaint is that sometimes KA over explains the people of the town. Almost every character you meet in the book you get a semi-description of and a little snippet from their lives. While I appreciate this sometimes it did seem a little overboard now and again. That said it did lend to the small town feel of the book and I get what she was trying to do but did I really need the police station receptionist’s backstory?<br /><br />Highly recommended to anyone who loves Romance and Suspense.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4685901288588519455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer314595533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5705818185972059414">Alrighty then! I just deleted yet another review accidentally. GOODREADS POWERS THAT BE: WE NEED A FREAKING AUTO-SAVE FEATURE FOR REVIEW DRAFTS!!! <br/><br/>Let me just say this: I liked this book, but I feel like there could have been a good 100 pages less of it. There was a lot of unnecessary everything. I also found it hard to believe that Colt, being the hard core alpha KA hero that he is, would let the love of his life leave him like she did without ANY explanation whatsoever. That right there lost a</span>
  <span id="freeText5705818185972059414" style="display:none">Alrighty then! I just deleted yet another review accidentally. GOODREADS POWERS THAT BE: WE NEED A FREAKING AUTO-SAVE FEATURE FOR REVIEW DRAFTS!!! <br><br>Let me just say this: I liked this book, but I feel like there could have been a good 100 pages less of it. There was a lot of unnecessary everything. I also found it hard to believe that Colt, being the hard core alpha KA hero that he is, would let the love of his life leave him like she did without ANY explanation whatsoever. That right there lost an entire star from me. Not at all feasible, and it didn't mesh with his character at all.<br><br>I DID love how the town features so prominently in the story. That's a classic Kristen Ashley plus right there. I didn't just read about this town...I lived there....<br><br>The sex is hot, the man is bossy, abrupt, and rough while still being gently and loving. <br><br>Feb is a great heroine....I love that she just threw her hands in the air and said <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375388i/729937.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Her town, in a way, betrayed her...so she left. But now she's back, and she's still in love with her man. He's still in love with her, and they are thrown together by a madman, forced to realize how short life is and how they've wasted twenty years holding on to some stupid grudge.<br><br>But in the end, these childhood sweethearts have loved each other since they were kids. And they don't waste any more time. Their love story is powerful, and I truly loved both Colt and Feb. Just because Colt is a bit overbearing doesn't mean Feb is weak. They compliment each other perfectly. There's nothing better than a happy ending for an unrequited love story!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375388i/729938.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5705818185972059414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=september-reads">september-reads</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer571574819" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11073578123302433757">I began this series not knowing what to expect, and once again KA produced a story that was full of action,suspence, romance, and of course; great sex! I am not usually fond of the reconcilliation stories; but this one I found was hard not to enjoy.<br/><br/>Colt and Februray fell in love at a young age and were the high school sweethearts that everyone knew would be together forever. Unfortuneatly, there was a MAJOR misunderstanding that was orchestrated by someone who was crazy and obsessed with Feb and</span>
  <span id="freeText11073578123302433757" style="display:none">I began this series not knowing what to expect, and once again KA produced a story that was full of action,suspence, romance, and of course; great sex! I am not usually fond of the reconcilliation stories; but this one I found was hard not to enjoy.<br /><br />Colt and Februray fell in love at a young age and were the high school sweethearts that everyone knew would be together forever. Unfortuneatly, there was a MAJOR misunderstanding that was orchestrated by someone who was crazy and obsessed with Feb and wanted her for himself. This caused Colt and Feb to go their seperate ways for many many years. What a tragedy, that two people who loved each other so much, end up missing out on all of that time together. They both married others, and had those marriages fail, but in the end fate brought them back together; but it was anything but smooth sailing for them. There is someone who is not done with Feb, he has had years to develop and continue his obsession; not only with Feb but with Colt too. Actually, this creep makes up this reality in his mind that he is Colt (Alec) and Feb is HIS.. Nothing will stop him from getting her back. In the process, he has a score to settle with the people who have wronged Feb...and this man wants to make these people pay with their lives.<br /><br />I loved this storyline, and I was very absorbed into it. My complaint was that it was so long, and there were sooo many characters introduced that it became hard to keep track of everyone and who they were. Other than that, there was never a dull moment, and it was impossible not to become absorbed into the lives of everyone in this little town. I look forward to the books that continue this series..Another successful series written by Kristen Ashley..</span>
  <a data-text-id="11073578123302433757" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1427493318" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1427493318" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=macho-protectors">macho-protectors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1427493318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13149247898419899437"><b>*** 3.85 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the KA addicts at the BB&B attic!!! </b><br/><br/>It has been two weeks since my last KA book and I had been jonezing for my doze! KA delivered as always. This book would be considered a second chance contemporary romance, and is a bit more subdued than the rest of her books, but apart from an explosion, it contained the usual damaged female with a good heart, the alpha male, who in this case happen NOT to be a jerk, a crazy murderous stalker, gunshots and the always mandatory ki</span>
  <span id="freeText13149247898419899437" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.85 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the KA addicts at the BB&amp;B attic!!! </b><br /><br />It has been two weeks since my last KA book and I had been jonezing for my doze! KA delivered as always. This book would be considered a second chance contemporary romance, and is a bit more subdued than the rest of her books, but apart from an explosion, it contained the usual damaged female with a good heart, the alpha male, who in this case happen NOT to be a jerk, a crazy murderous stalker, gunshots and the always mandatory kidnapping. It would not be a KA book without it:-)<br /><br />This book is one of those that make me want to grab the editing machete and slice off at least 100-150 pages of details, which though helping with setting the mood of the very small town, feel redundant and superfluous at times... But even with them, KA can still wrap you up in her stories with the elusive magic that is all her own. It is a solid beginning for the Burg Series. <br /><br />I liked Colt, but Fab was not my favorite female lead by KA. She was too needy to be strong, which I think we were supposed to percive her as. However, the plot was solid, the secondary characters had depth, and we got what we always expect from this author - a teary, but syrupy sweet Happily Ever After:-) As long as she keeps delivering those, I am a fan for life! <br /><br />If you like an adult contemporary romance with some justice delivered to some bad people, this is the book for you! Not for the very young readers, a bit too much S&amp;V. <br /><br />Now I wish you all Happy Reading and may you never run out of good books!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13149247898419899437" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Kristen Ashley, reunion romances, &amp; dark, creepy suspense</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame">hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-alpha%E2%80%8E">hero-alpha‎</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=childhood-ties-friends-sweethearts">childhood-ties-friends-sweethearts</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268029896" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8788792533645974473">4 stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>I’m an avid Kristen Ashley fan, but this isn’t my favorite of her books. And although I didn’t enjoy it as much as the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> and <i>Dream Man</i> series, <i>
  <b>For You</b>
</i> is still a good read. <br/><br/>KA’s writing style tends to be very detailed, descriptive, and lengthy, and it just didn’t work as well for me this time. It’s a great second chance romance with a likable H/h and dark, chilling suspense elements, but it felt bogged down at times, which kept </span>
  <span id="freeText8788792533645974473" style="display:none">4 stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br /><br />I’m an avid Kristen Ashley fan, but this isn’t my favorite of her books. And although I didn’t enjoy it as much as the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> and <i>Dream Man</i> series, <i>
  <b>For You</b>
</i> is still a good read. <br /><br />KA’s writing style tends to be very detailed, descriptive, and lengthy, and it just didn’t work as well for me this time. It’s a great second chance romance with a likable H/h and dark, chilling suspense elements, but it felt bogged down at times, which kept it from being as gripping and taut of a thriller as it could’ve been. It took a hell of a long time for the big secret that kept February and Colt apart to be revealed, and the plot meandered too much, which hindered the overall story a bit. <br /><br />But the emotional, passionate romance between Feb and Colt and its intense, thrilling climax and gratifying HEA ending compensated for the slower parts of the story. So while not my favorite, this still deserves a solid 4 stars. <br /><br />I’ve already bought the other books in <i>The ‘Burg</i> series, and I’m still happily full steam ahead on the KA train!<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1134987998" />
    <a title="Sher❤ The Fabulous BookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5493776-sher-the-fabulous-booklover"><img alt="Sher❤ The Fabulous BookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546387092p2/5493776.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer13322587026404927580"><b>**4 Solid Stars**</b><br/><br/>I don't even know where to start with this one. This book was definitely on crack. And by that I mean it pretty much had everything:<br/><br/>-Murder<br/>-Mystery and Intrigue<br/>-Romance<br/>-Dead bodies piling up<br/>-Crazy, ax killing Stalker/Murderer <br/>-Close knit Family<br/>-Sexy, hot Alpha Male<br/><br/>For you is a story about two high school sweethearts, February Owens and Alec Colton, who are brought together by a tragic circumstance.   <span id="freeText13322587026404927580" style="display:none"><b>**4 Solid Stars**</b><br /><br />I don't even know where to start with this one. This book was definitely on crack. And by that I mean it pretty much had everything:<br /><br />-Murder<br />-Mystery and Intrigue<br />-Romance<br />-Dead bodies piling up<br />-Crazy, ax killing Stalker/Murderer <br />-Close knit Family<br />-Sexy, hot Alpha Male<br /><br />For you is a story about two high school sweethearts, February Owens and Alec Colton, who are brought together by a tragic circumstance. This was filled with so much action and suspense that at one point I totally forgot I was reading a KA novel! I loved it and no one writes a better alpha male in my opinion. <br /><br />For You is an amazing start of the series and I can't wait to read the rest. If you want a book that's romance but keeps you on the edge of your seat then you'd enjoy this.</span>
