<div id="review_1498738126" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1498738126" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1498738126?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of the author</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2016_reads">2016_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1498738126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10756811123309980374">It pains me to say this but some of these KA books are just too freakin' long. Where is a good editor when you need one? Sometimes I don't mind the endless details but in this story, which is a romantic suspense, I thought the endless details and introduction of <i>so many</i> characters not essential to the story (and giving them lines to speak) helped to slow down the momentum of the story. I want my RS to move at a fast pace, with me dying to turn the page to find out what will happen. But sadly, th</span>
  <span id="freeText10756811123309980374" style="display:none">It pains me to say this but some of these KA books are just too freakin' long. Where is a good editor when you need one? Sometimes I don't mind the endless details but in this story, which is a romantic suspense, I thought the endless details and introduction of <i>so many</i> characters not essential to the story (and giving them lines to speak) helped to slow down the momentum of the story. I want my RS to move at a fast pace, with me dying to turn the page to find out what will happen. But sadly, there were times with this one that I was dying to turn the page--just to skip some parts and move the story forward.<br /><br />Don't get me wrong, this was not a dud at all. I liked the whole RS plot idea (except I hate hate hate when the H/h break up over something they<i> think </i>they witnessed or heard, without<i> talking</i> about what they witnessed. I hate the whole big misunderstanding thing, especially when it drags on for 20 years! And when either the H/h remains messed up for all that time. Which btw, also happened in a similar way in another KA book (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24199806.Walk_Through_Fire__Chaos___4_" title="Walk Through Fire (Chaos, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Walk Through Fire</a>). So I had to put my dislike of that particular trope behind, and try to move on with the story.<br /><br />It helped that KA gave us a particularly swoonworthy hero in police detective Alec 'Colt' Colton. I loved him. It took me a while to warm up to bar owner February Owens though. Not exactly sure why. But as the story progressed I liked her more and more and respected her. I guess I liked that their relationship before they got together wasn't mean or antagonistic like with some other KA couples.<br /><br />KA created a really sick villain. And what he did to his victims and what he put our H/h through was just sick, twisted, and gruesome. But why oh why, when the police and Feds knew this serial killer was coming for them, why weren't they better protected? One off-duty cop to protect them? Plus friends and family members? I dunno, I feel like their bar should've been swarming with feds...<br /><br />Good points? The chemistry and history between Feb and Alec. KA never stumbles over this. They had heat, passion, and a great back story.<br />The gripping climax--once we finally got to it! And of course the HEA--KA never fails on giving good, satisfying HEAs.:)<br /><br />To sum up: this story had 500+ pages. That's a lot to carry for a RS. I wish this story had about 100 pages edited out. I would rather be left with wanting more from a story, than wondering when it is going to wrap up. So sort of a lukewarm thumbs up from me. 3 1/2 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="10756811123309980374" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_281320451" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/281320451" />
    <a title="Searock" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6641663-searock"><img alt="Searock" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396402019p2/6641663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/281320451?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Searock" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Searock" href="/user/show/6641663-searock">Searock</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun">my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer281320451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9171867563075585323">4.75 stars<br/>I may have to get back to you for a review...<br/>(I'm in the glow)<br/><br/>Oh wait, turns out I have something after all!<br/>(hope you don't mind that I won't be getting very specific about any of it)<br/><br/>This story was full-bodied with plenty of detail, a full cast of characters, good story structure and the writing simply flowed.<br/><b>The reading of it was utterly fulfilling</b>.<br/>Scenes were in turns full of despair and longing, hypnotic, witty, delightful, sensual and intimate. <br/>The writing truly had flashes of bril</span>
  <span id="freeText9171867563075585323" style="display:none">4.75 stars<br />I may have to get back to you for a review...<br />(I'm in the glow)<br /><br />Oh wait, turns out I have something after all!<br />(hope you don't mind that I won't be getting very specific about any of it)<br /><br />This story was full-bodied with plenty of detail, a full cast of characters, good story structure and the writing simply flowed.<br /><b>The reading of it was utterly fulfilling</b>.<br />Scenes were in turns full of despair and longing, hypnotic, witty, delightful, sensual and intimate. <br />The writing truly had flashes of brilliance. <br />KA is getting even more extraordinary at this writing gig. <br />It looks absolutely effortless.<br />I can't even describe the point of view off the top of my head. I think it was first person from a both the leads, but felt at times, omniscient in that I didn't feel stuck in someone's head or limited by any lack of perspective.<br /><br />Like in many KA novels, <b>the supporting cast is big, delightful and surprisingly well realized</b>. I don't know how she does it! Even the cat who was referred to maybe 6 times, was a compelling character who had a wonderful, symbolic role in the story. I have a theory about the name of the cat, "Wilson", which is probably completely false. Hmmm. Anyway, another great side character is one of February's (h) former love interests (there are a few). He has very limited page space yet the way he's written is powerful (how you do that, KA?). Another background character who works at a restaurant who is never actually seen "on screen" until the last chapter has a freaking story arc. It's a teeny tiny little arc and its just symbolic in nature, but delightful nonetheless. <br /><i>There should be like, an award for that or something, right?</i> <br /><br />The story is constantly in <b>forward motion</b>. Any reflection on the past simply reveals information. There is an organic ever-unfolding nature to the writing that I adore. Lots of scenes, lots of relationships, lots of intriguing back story that's revealed over time.<br /><br />Only one little bit that niggles: <br />First of all, I am not a huge fan of suspense. <br />This book has a suspenseful plot line, but it is believable and really well-done. I love that it does not overshadow or choke the story but actually enhances it, drives the plot forward and serves to reveal lots of characterization. That said, KA often has heroines confront the "enemy/ghost from the past/ex-something/abuser/kidnapper" etc. at some point in her books. It's not that I mind it and in some stories I love it, but in this book I simply didn't believe it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When someone is a completely insane, psychotic, mass-murdering maniac, and he is wielding an axe, is that really a good time to have a lengthy emotional discussion with him (there are cops with guns pointed at him at the time, but still). Seemed far fetched that she would attempt to get him to see the light at that moment. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Compared to the awesomeness of the rest of this delicious piece of love, that was a blip on the screen. I wholeheartedly look forward to the next one.<br /><br />One thing that may be notable: I put this book down. Alot. At the time of this review, I haven't decided whether it was because I didn't "have to know" what happened next or I was putting off finishing for not wanting it to be over. I definitely savored a few chapters at a time. I didn't read any other books between, but I did other things. I honestly think it might be related to the suspense element. Suspense makes me uncomfortable no matter the intensity. I am a wuss. This all changed in the last chapters though and I couldn't stop reading. <br /><br />The final chapter that follows the climax reads like an epilogue (which KA does like no other!) and it's so very satisfying. Arcs are completed. Secondary relationships are visited. There is something so special and delightful about that last chapter. I just can't describe it.<br /><br />*continues basking*</span>
  <a data-text-id="9171867563075585323" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_329834956" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/329834956" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/329834956?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer329834956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5538645545004149015"><b>3.5 Stars</b>…This was my first Kristen Ashley read and it was just as sexy as I thought it would be! KA's writing is unique to anything I've read before; the dialogue is down to earth and gives you a feel of comfort and closeness with the characters. <br/><br/>The story was interesting and had a romantic-suspense theme. The highly psychotic murderer on the loose added an exciting and creepy twist that I enjoyed. There was so much terrific build up at the start of book that I expected to be completely floored</span>
  <span id="freeText5538645545004149015" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b>…This was my first Kristen Ashley read and it was just as sexy as I thought it would be! KA's writing is unique to anything I've read before; the dialogue is down to earth and gives you a feel of comfort and closeness with the characters. <br><br>The story was interesting and had a romantic-suspense theme. The highly psychotic murderer on the loose added an exciting and creepy twist that I enjoyed. There was so much terrific build up at the start of book that I expected to be completely floored when everything eventually came to a head, but unfortunately, the element of suspense ended up falling just a little flat. I also feel that the story dragged at certain parts, and could have benefited from being a big shorter. <br><br>I must admit that the relationship between February and Colt was fire-hot! KA, no doubt, knows how to write a five-star love scene. There was the ever-famous sexual tension present in the beginning which evolved shamelessly into raw, sexual heat. If you're into erotic-romance, do not deny yourself a Kristen Ashley love scene!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Adult Comtemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Rekindled love. Intense connection.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Down-to-earth, spunky. Alpha hero. Strong heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> A love that never died is rekindled as hero desperately tries to protect heroine from a crazed stalker. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Wordy. Blunt. Slightly disjointed, but creates natural feel in dialogue. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Spinoff<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer410106221" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17172341806010867565"><br/><b>YOU CAN'T REWRITE HISTORY! </b><br/><br/>In this town, EVERYONE knew that February Owens and Alexander Colton were meant to be.<br/><br/><b>“Romeo and Juliet, say they didn’t die but Juliet got pissed and took off. Everyone would know it was Romeo and Juliet, would always be Romeo and Juliet, even if later Romeo hooked up with Nancy. No one ever heard of Nancy, doesn’t even sound right, Romeo and Nancy. Everyone knows Romeo’s meant to be with Juliet. Even if Romeo loved Nancy, Nancy would always know she was never Juliet.</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17172341806010867565" style="display:none"><br /><b>YOU CAN'T REWRITE HISTORY! </b><br /><br />In this town, EVERYONE knew that February Owens and Alexander Colton were meant to be.<br /><br /><b>“Romeo and Juliet, say they didn’t die but Juliet got pissed and took off. Everyone would know it was Romeo and Juliet, would always be Romeo and Juliet, even if later Romeo hooked up with Nancy. No one ever heard of Nancy, doesn’t even sound right, Romeo and Nancy. Everyone knows Romeo’s meant to be with Juliet. Even if Romeo loved Nancy, Nancy would always know she was never Juliet.”</b><br /><br />Alexander Colton and February Owens have been in love with each other their whole lives. <br /><br /><b> “Since I was three, there’s never been a day when I wasn’t in love with you.”</b> <br /><br />Outside forces play an evil part in their relationship’s demise leaving February and Alec without each other for twenty-two years.<br /> <br />The same evil force that destroyed their relationship returns with a vengeance to rewrite history tossing Alec and February together. They fall back into place with ease. <br /><br /><b>“ I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried.”</b> <br /><br />A scary read and a lot of lives lost but true love as in Feb and Alec prevail!<br /><br /><b>“He’s gone now. Now it’s just you and me and the life we were meant to have.” </b> <br /></span>

<div id="review_1625578170" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1625578170" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1625578170?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1625578170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1003177149417727707">Another KA buddy-read with the crazy chicks at the BBB group. If you want to join a really fun group, and you're a little neurotic, we are here for you!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462081481i/18950972.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>And, then join the Buddies Books and Baubles group!</i><br/><br/>So, we read these Kristen Ashley books and they all have a sort of feel to them. There is always an alpha-male who may or may not be pushing the boundaries of assholeness. There is always some sort of danger that the female gets into. The females have a tendency to whisper. (I don't know why.). T</span>
  <span id="freeText1003177149417727707" style="display:none">Another KA buddy-read with the crazy chicks at the BBB group. If you want to join a really fun group, and you're a little neurotic, we are here for you!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462081481i/18950972.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>And, then join the Buddies Books and Baubles group!</i><br><br>So, we read these Kristen Ashley books and they all have a sort of feel to them. There is always an alpha-male who may or may not be pushing the boundaries of assholeness. There is always some sort of danger that the female gets into. The females have a tendency to whisper. (I don't know why.). There is always at least one kidnapping. Outfits are described and often songs are mentioned. And, insta-love abounds. If you can deal with all of that, you will have fun because there is also always humor.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462081481i/18950973.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book has a second-chance love story. Our heroes are actually kind of old for the genre - 42 &amp; 44, but have known each other since they were 3 &amp; 5 years old. They were high school sweethearts, but suddenly broke up when he was in college and we don't learn the reason why for a good part of the book. And, believe me, it's annoying because a conversation or two would have fixed it. But, noooo, they both married other people and went about their lives apart for over 20 years.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462081481i/18950974._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>misunderstandings always cause great pain!</i><br><br>So, we have Colt/Alec who is a detective, and February who is the part-owner of a bar. They avoid each other at all costs until a murder brings them back together. The murderer is fixated on February and Colt intends on keeping her safe.<br><br>As one security expert puts it:<br><b>
  <i>"It would suck you two finally being back together only for one of you to end up hacked up with a hatchet."</i>
</b><br><br>That would put a damper on things. Thank you, Captain Obvious!<br><br>So, we have a pretty good crime story with a creepy killer, and the romance going on. I enjoyed both parts of it because this alpha-guy wasn't a big ole asshole for once. And, the murderer guy was pretty evil and sick. I like sick and evil. Sometimes the bad guy will only kill one person, or be someone who kills for reasons. I can't really sink my teeth into those kind. I want a villain who is going to be seriously screwed-up and bloodthirsty. If we are going for a bad guy, go all the way. Make me happy that the book is fiction!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462081481i/18950975.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> I know! It's so hard to get good evil minions these days!</i><br><br>Because of the great bad guy, and the non-asshole alpha, this was probably one of my favorite KA books. I'm excited to continue the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1003177149417727707" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_280351212" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280351212" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280351212?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=lost-love-rekindled">lost-love-rekindled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cop-hero">cop-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=serial-killer">serial-killer</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280351212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11918310602043460954">Book 1 in the Burgs Series which Kristen Ashley refers to as a ‘crime’ series on her website. It is in fact an edgy romantic suspense with a sadistic hatchet wielding homicidal maniac on the prowl with February Owens (our heroine) as his object of desire and will stop at nothing to avenge the wrongs he perceives have been done to her over the years. And we are talking years here – he carves up someone she once had an argument with at high school right at the beginning of the novel.<br/>He leaves this</span>
  <span id="freeText11918310602043460954" style="display:none">Book 1 in the Burgs Series which Kristen Ashley refers to as a ‘crime’ series on her website. It is in fact an edgy romantic suspense with a sadistic hatchet wielding homicidal maniac on the prowl with February Owens (our heroine) as his object of desire and will stop at nothing to avenge the wrongs he perceives have been done to her over the years. And we are talking years here – he carves up someone she once had an argument with at high school right at the beginning of the novel.<br />He leaves this body at the back of the bar Feb works in and part owns with her brother Morrie for her to discover. Enter stage left – Lieutenant Alexander Colton – our hero. He’s a cop and is called to the scene. Alec ‘Colt’ and February have a long history which is drip fed to us slowly through the book. They were high school sweethearts and broke up due to a ‘big misunderstanding’ and Feb went off the rails allegedly sleeping with every guy in town. They both married other people – Feb’s marriage ending when her husband beat and attempted to rape her. Colt exacted a physical revenge on Feb’s bottom –dwelling pond sludge of an ex and Feb left town.<br />15 lonely years later, Feb returns to town to help run the bar with Morrie now that her parents have retired and studiously avoids the newly-divorced Colt for a couple of years until her world explodes when our killer starts his work and Colt wades in to protect her.<br />Kristen Ashley really does write suspense well with the killer an ever present threat lurking ominously. He’s totally psychotic and sadistic and reminded me very much of a Karen Rose villain although the book is way sexier than a KR novel,<br />It’s also a great romance – you can tell that fate intends for these two to be together. They’ve been totally unable to find happiness with anyone else but circumstance has intervened to keep them asunder for years. Colt even speculates that they can be happier now because of this….<br /><br /><i>Then in my ear, he said, “I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried.” I sucked in breath, unprepared for this stealth attack, while he went on. “Who knows, baby? We had all that time together, I coulda got used to it, learned to take it for granted.” His arms gave me a squeeze. “Now, that’ll never happen.”</i><br /><br />Le sigh. Colt is wonderful – he’s totally genuine, caring, protective and very, very hot. They really set the pages on fire with this one. February is, at first, very reserved, unwilling to let Colt back in but you know she’s always been in love with him and it’s just a matter of time and I adored how they loved each other. They’ve a lot of history together and this is very much a story of a love once lost, refound and rekindled.<br /><br />Fabulous.<br /><br />5 stars romantic suspense.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11918310602043460954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14137411209325554326">For You was amazing, but it’s Kristen Ashley, so that’s not surprising. Loved everything about it! <br/><br/>February and Colt had such a heartbreaking history and you could feel the longing and sadness between these two when the story opened. Colt is like a member of the family, taken in under February’s family’s love and protection since he was five. From there Feb has always been in love with him, even during their long years apart, same thing with Colt. They were childhood and high school sweethearts </span>
  <span id="freeText14137411209325554326" style="display:none">For You was amazing, but it’s Kristen Ashley, so that’s not surprising. Loved everything about it! <br /><br />February and Colt had such a heartbreaking history and you could feel the longing and sadness between these two when the story opened. Colt is like a member of the family, taken in under February’s family’s love and protection since he was five. From there Feb has always been in love with him, even during their long years apart, same thing with Colt. They were childhood and high school sweethearts until they weren’t when Feb abruptly breaks up with Colt, when she’s twenty and he’s twenty-two. They lead their separate lives, both getting married and then divorced to other people, but Feb’s back in town for the last two years, helping her brother run their family’s bar after their parents retire. As a reader, you know, <i>just know</i> these two are on a path towards each other, and fortunately Kristen Ashley doesn’t make you wait too long. <br /><br />A murdered woman turns up at the back of the bar and then a sinister note points at Feb being in the center of the killer’s mind. Little does Feb and Colt know, they’ve been the center of his focus for years. Colt is determined to protect Feb, never mind their history, and in doing so something beautiful starts to happen again, making me one HAPPY READER!!<br /><b><br />“Like it right now or not, Feb, coupla days ago, you gave yourself back to me. You think I’m letting that go, think again because, baby, you’re fucking <i>wrong</i>.”<br /><br />“I remember everything about you and I remember all the reasons why I loved you. Never could forget even when I tried.”</b><br /><br />Chilling facts come out and danger is all around making this a suspenseful read, leading up to a heart-stopping final showdown! Between the oh-so-sweet romance, the revelations, and the suspense, I didn’t want to put this book down. This is a long book, but I was not bored for even one of those pages. Love Kristen Ashley! Love her strong Alpha males! She is the Queen of writing Alpha males, but also the Queen of writing loveable, spunky heroines. Colt and February are no exception! <br /><br />I finished this novel with a few tears in my eyes and my heart soaring! <br /><b><br />“One thing,” I said into his chest, “one thing that’s good, Colt, and that is, every day, for all these years, I thought of you, dozens of times a day. Every day. Every single <i>fucking</i> day.”<br />“February,” Colt whispered. <br />“Still do, except, now…it doesn’t hurt anymore.”</b><br /></span>

  <b>“Romeo and Juliet, say they didn’t die but Juliet got pissed and took off. Something about it, not sure what, just had me putting it off till last!<br /><br />No idea why once I read it!<br /><br />A bit more romance suspense than some of her other series. Not as light-hearted.<br /><br />But, this book has an awesome couple of main characters. I loved Colt and Feb and loved them together.<br /><br />An excellent cast of secondary characters.<br /><br />A great plot, filled with secrets and lies and murder.<br /><br />And above all, a beautiful bitter-sweet story of two people who were destined to be, yet had not been, lived with the pain and found their way back to each other! <br /><br /><br />While there is some drama and mystery going on, it is very much a character and relationship driven story! You were very much invested in these two getting their HEA, whilst also finding yourself really caring about the secondary characters and their lives!<br /><br />Remains an excellent 5 stars!<br /><br /><i>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_330150008" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/330150008" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/330150008?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=mystery-suspense">mystery-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=actiony">actiony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer330150008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16745925936651852096">A gorgeously hot ultra-protective guy reunited with his gorgeously hot but messed up first love 22 years after she broke his heart and he never knew why. Throw in a brilliant cast of family and friends, the usual KA banter, steam and swooniness and one freaky as all hell serial killer, and you have utter perfection!<br/><br/>OK, I had to give myself some time to contain the gush-fest that I would have written immediately after finishing the book, but I’ve managed to calm down, and am able to restrain myse</span>
  <span id="freeText16745925936651852096" style="display:none">A gorgeously hot ultra-protective guy reunited with his gorgeously hot but messed up first love 22 years after she broke his heart and he never knew why. Throw in a brilliant cast of family and friends, the usual KA banter, steam and swooniness and one freaky as all hell serial killer, and you have utter perfection!<br /><br />OK, I had to give myself some time to contain the gush-fest that I would have written immediately after finishing the book, but I’ve managed to calm down, and am able to restrain myself (at least a little bit), so here goes.<br /><br />Feb is a lost soul who has returned to her home town after 15 years of aimless wandering while trying to hide from mistakes in her past. Colt is a stable, respected detective, and the local eye candy. Oh, and he’s also absolutely incredible!! He’s everything you would possibly want in a guy, but without the usual OTT-Alpha that you see in a lot of other KA heroes (not that I’m complaining in any way, because we all love that as well!!!). They have been avoiding each other for the two years since Feb's return, but the chemistry between these two is intense - childhood sweethearts who are still in love with each other after all of these years apart. <br /><br />The POV alternates between Feb and Colt, which I loved, because we get to see not only what they’re going through now, but also their perceptions of what happened in the past to tear these two apart and how they dealt with it. The back-part of the story unravels slowly, and you get clues along the way that help you piece it all together. <br /><br />The inevitable reunion is realistic and oh-so-swoony (and pretty freaking hot as well - whew!), and there are some very intense scenes as they come to realise exactly what happened to tear them apart, and then figure out how to move forward. What I really loved about their relationship was that they both accepted fault for how it all went down, and then they didn’t dwell on it. It happened, but looking back and wishing wasn’t going to change anything, so they were both prepared to put it behind them and move on. And even though the intense connection had been there between them all along, they recognised that who you are as a person at 20 is completely different from who you are at 40, so it was useless trying to pick up exactly where they left off. They just needed to move on and start fresh - and I loved that! <br /><br />The serial killer storyline is horrific and creepy. The killer is fixated on Feb, and reading how this affected her and Colt was both devastating and beautiful as they were inexorably drawn to each other – Feb turning to Colt for support and Colt just wanting to protect his girl (awwww).<br /><br />Throughout all of the drama though there are some very funny moments, and a great cast of characters. I loved that the whole town was cheering for their reunion and watching everything unfold - cell phones in hand, ready to capture any little moments. And that Feb and Colt both knew it and totally didn't care! <br /><br />The usual KA-end-of-book-climax is intense and tragic; my heart was racing while reading it. And as for the HEA - well it was pretty freaking epic. Not only did we get a gorgeously swoony story come to completion, but all of the characters that we came to love throughout the story are involved, so we get to see their reactions to the events as well. The whole thing left me bouncing up and down and squeeing like an idiot. <br /><br />Like anyone who reads KA books, I am forever a die hard fan and will read anything she writes (seriously, I’d read her grocery list at this point and get excited over it), and it struck me again in this book just how brilliant her writing is. KA depicts her scenes so vividly, she puts you right in the scene with her characters, and you can feel all of the emotion and picture it all happening as if it was right in front of you. It makes for some heart-wrenching reading, but the intensely emotional scenes that she writes are part of the reason I love her books so much. She’s a master. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16745925936651852096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

They will leave you drooling every time and wishing that you were in the book with them. <div id="review_566707238" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/566707238" />
    <a title="Mistress" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5511876-mistress"><img alt="Mistress" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383055853p2/5511876.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/566707238?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mistress" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mistress" href="/user/show/5511876-mistress">Mistress</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer566707238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13732849459280895884">Well... how can I put this nicely? This book was ok. I wonder if it was just me because KA usually is so good, but I really couldn't get into this one. It seemed like the never ending story to me. I had to force myself to finish this book. It wasn't bad, but it wasn't really good, IMO. I was so bored through the whole book. Halfway through I just wanted the bad guy to hack up everyone with his hatchet and be done with it. I liked the "KA speak"... you know where the men only talk in half sentenc</span>
  <span id="freeText13732849459280895884" style="display:none">Well... how can I put this nicely? This book was ok. I wonder if it was just me because KA usually is so good, but I really couldn't get into this one. It seemed like the never ending story to me. I had to force myself to finish this book. It wasn't bad, but it wasn't really good, IMO. I was so bored through the whole book. Halfway through I just wanted the bad guy to hack up everyone with his hatchet and be done with it. I liked the "KA speak"... you know where the men only talk in half sentences and grunts, in the Dream Man series because it fit with the tough bad boy persona, but in this book everyone, male and female, talked like that. It was too much. I also hated how they always interrupted each other by saying the other person's name. Colt... Colt... Colt... Colt... Feb... Feb... Feb... Feb... It drove me insane! I just wanted the hatchet man to show up and end their dumb conversations in a bloody massacre. At least then I might not be bored to tears. So, needless to say this is not one I would really recommend even for KA lovers. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382325914i/5820897.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382325914i/5820898.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13732849459280895884" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QprmGrp97nvvXbAqgUuO4bQSimib9RVsaKLqx7D6qh81S/TGUL9dlIcZtGsPgR1Q2oqFgg2EWitp5tBf2sWckA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kBG/YGBjNn9H+ak5nAj8f8UFq0bRQexyUIQwO/B+P+XnwK28iqGFkC+9rXgSwm/Oq52krEcwozVRwAqjmkEJag==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText16370315508996434012" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
